<s> egypt's economy was highly centralized during the rule of former president gamal abdel nasser but has opened up considerably under former president anwar el-sadat and current president mohamed hosni mubarak <\s>
<s> cairo from 2004 to 2008 aggressively pursued economic reforms to attract foreign investment and facilitate gdp growth <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis has slowed the reform efforts <\s>
<s> the budget deficit climbed to over 8 of gdp and egypt's gdp growth slowed to 4.6 in 2009 predominately due to reduced growth in export-oriented sectors including manufacturing and tourism and suez canal revenues <\s>
<s> in 2010 the government spent more on infrastructure and public projects and exports drove gdp growth to more than 5 but gdp growth in 2011 is unlikely to bounce back to pre-global financial recession levels when it stood at 7 <\s>
<s> despite the relatively high levels of economic growth over the past few years living conditions for the average egyptian remain poor <\s>
<s> el salvador despite being the smallest country geographically in central america el salvador has the third largest economy in the region <\s>
<s> the economy took a hit from the global recession and real gdp contracted by 3.5 in 2009 <\s>
<s> the economy began a slow recovery in 2010 on the back of improved export and remittances figures <\s>
<s> remittances accounted for 16 of gdp in 2009 and about a third of all households receive these transfers <\s>
<s> in 2006 el salvador was the first country to ratify the dominican republic-central american free trade agreement cafta-dr which has bolstered the export of processed foods sugar and ethanol and supported investment in the apparel sector amid increased asian competition and the expiration of the multi-fiber agreement in 2005 <\s>
<s> el salvador has promoted an open trade and investment environment and has embarked on a wave of privatizations extending to telecom electricity distribution banking and pension funds <\s>
<s> in late 2006 the government and the millennium challenge corporation signed a five-year 461 million compact to stimulate economic growth and reduce poverty in the country's northern region the primary conflict zone during the civil war through investments in education public services enterprise development and transportation infrastructure <\s>
<s> with the adoption of the us dollar as its currency in 2001 el salvador lost control over monetary policy <\s>
<s> any counter-cyclical policy response to the downturn must be through fiscal policy which is constrained by legislative requirements for a two-thirds majority to approve any international financing <\s>
<s> equatorial guinea the discovery and exploitation of large oil reserves have contributed to dramatic economic growth but fluctuating oil prices have produced huge swings in gdp growth in recent years <\s>
<s> forestry farming and fishing are also major components of gdp <\s>
<s> subsistence farming is the dominate form of livelihood <\s>
<s> although pre-independence equatorial guinea counted on cocoa production for hard currency earnings the neglect of the rural economy under successive regimes has diminished potential for agriculture-led growth the government has stated its intention to reinvest some oil revenue into agriculture <\s>
<s> a number of aid programs sponsored by the world bank and the imf have been cut off since 1993 because of corruption and mismanagement <\s>
<s> government officials and their family members own most businesses but corruption is rampant <\s>
<s> undeveloped natural resources include titanium iron ore manganese uranium and alluvial gold <\s>
<s> growth remained strong in 2008 led by oil but dropped in 2009-10 as the price of oil fell <\s>
<s> eritrea since independence from ethiopia in 1993 eritrea has faced the economic problems of a small desperately poor country accentuated by the recent implementation of restrictive economic policies <\s>
<s> eritrea has a command economy under the control of the sole political party the people's front for democracy and justice pfdj <\s>
<s> like the economies of many african nations a large share of the population nearly 80 is engaged in subsistence agriculture but they produce only a small share of total output <\s>
<s> since the conclusion of the ethiopian-eritrea war in 2000 the government has maintained a firm grip on the economy expanding the use of the military and party-owned businesses to complete eritrea's development agenda <\s>
<s> the government strictly controls the use of foreign currency by limiting access and availability <\s>
<s> few private enterprises remain in eritrea <\s>
<s> eritrea's economy depends heavily on taxes paid by members of the diaspora <\s>
<s> erratic rainfall and the delayed demobilization of agriculturalists from the military continue to interfere with agricultural production and eritrea's recent harvests have been unable to meet the food needs of the country <\s>
<s> the government continues to place its hope for additional revenue on the development of several international mining projects <\s>
<s> despite difficulties for international companies in working with the eritrean government a canadian mining company signed a contract with the government in 2007 and began mineral extraction in 2010 <\s>
<s> eritrea's economic future depends upon its ability to master social problems such as illiteracy unemployment and low skills and more importantly on the government's willingness to support a true market economy <\s>
<s> nevertheless the economy in the area under government control has grown at a rate well above the eu average since 2000 <\s>
<s> cyprus joined the european exchange rate mechanism erm 2 in may 2005 and adopted the euro as its national currency on 1 january 2008 <\s>
<s> an aggressive austerity program in the preceding years aimed at paving the way for the euro helped turn a soaring fiscal deficit 6.3 in 2003 into a surplus of 1.2 in 2008 and reduced inflation to 4.7 <\s>
<s> this prosperity came under pressure in 2009 as construction and tourism slowed in the face of reduced foreign demand triggered by the ongoing global financial crisis <\s>
<s> although cyprus lagged its eu peers in showing signs of stress from the global crisis the economy tipped into recession in mid 2009 and contracted 1.8 for the year <\s>
<s> in addition the budget deficit is on the rise and reached 5.7 of gdp in 2010 a violation of the eu's budget deficit criteria of no more than 3 of gdp <\s>
<s> in response to the country's deteriorating finances nicosia is promising to implement measures to cut the cost of the state payroll curb tax evasion and revamp social benefits <\s>
<s> however it has been slow to act lacking a consensus in parliament and among the social partners for its proposed measures <\s>
<s> czech republic the czech republic is one of the most stable and prosperous of the post-communist states of central and eastern europe <\s>
<s> maintaining an open investment climate has been a key element of the czech republic's transition from a communist centrally planned economy to a functioning market economy <\s>
<s> as a member of the european union with an advantageous location in the center of europe a relatively low cost structure and a well-qualified labor force the czech republic is an attractive destination for foreign investment <\s>
<s> prior to its eu accession in 2004 the czech government harmonized its laws and regulations with those of the european union <\s>
<s> the small open export-driven czech economy grew by over 6 annually from 2005-2007 and by 2.5 in 2008 <\s>
<s> the conservative czech financial system has remained relatively healthy throughout 2009 <\s>
<s> nevertheless the real economy contracted by 4.1 in 2009 mainly due to a significant drop in external demand as the czech republic's main export markets fell into recession <\s>
<s> gdp is expected to grow by 2.4 in 2010 driven largely by a rebound in external demand particularly from gremany <\s>
<s> denmark this thoroughly modern market economy features a high-tech agricultural sector state-of-the-art industry with world-leading firms in pharmaceuticals maritime shipping and renewable energy and a high dependence on foreign trade <\s>
<s> the danish economy is also characterized by extensive government welfare measures an equitable distribution of income and comfortable living standards <\s>
<s> denmark is a net exporter of food and energy and enjoys a comfortable balance of payments surplus <\s>
<s> after a long consumption-driven upswing denmark's economy began slowing in 2007 with the end of a housing boom <\s>
<s> housing prices dropped markedly in 2008-09 <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis has exacerbated this cyclical slowdown through increased borrowing costs and lower export demand consumer confidence and investment <\s>
<s> the global financial crises cut danish gdp by 0.9 in 2008 and 4.7 in 2009 <\s>
<s> historically low levels of unemployment rose sharply with the recession but remain below 5 about half the level of the eu <\s>
<s> denmark made a modest recovery in 2010 in part because of increased government spending <\s>
<s> an impending decline in the ratio of workers to retirees will be a major long-term issue <\s>
<s> denmark maintained a healthy budget surplus for many years up to 2008 but the budget balance swung into deficit during 2009-10 <\s>
<s> nonetheless denmark's fiscal position remains among the strongest in the eu <\s>
<s> despite previously meeting the criteria to join the european economic and monetary union emu so far denmark has decided not to join although the danish krone remains pegged to the euro <\s>
<s> dhekelia economic activity is limited to providing services to the military and their families located in dhekelia <\s>
<s> all food and manufactured goods must be imported <\s>
<s> djibouti the economy is based on service activities connected with the country's strategic location and status as a free trade zone in the horn of africa <\s>
<s> two-thirds of djibouti's inhabitants live in the capital city the remainder are mostly nomadic herders <\s>
<s> scanty rainfall limits crop production to fruits and vegetables and most food must be imported <\s>
<s> djibouti provides services as both a transit port for the region and an international transshipment and refueling center <\s>
<s> imports and exports from landlocked neighbor ethiopia represent 70 of port activity at djibouti's container terminal <\s>
<s> djibouti has few natural resources and little industry <\s>
<s> the nation is therefore heavily dependent on foreign assistance to help support its balance of payments and to finance development projects <\s>
<s> an unemployment rate of nearly 60 in urban areas continues to be a major problem <\s>
<s> while inflation is not a concern due to the fixed tie of the djiboutian franc to the us dollar the artificially high value of the djiboutian franc adversely affects djibouti's balance of payments <\s>
<s> per capita consumption dropped an estimated 35 between 1999 and 2006 because of recession civil war and a high population growth rate including immigrants and refugees <\s>
<s> djibouti has experienced relatively minimal impact from the global economic downturn but its reliance on diesel-generated electricity and imported food leave average consumers vulnerable to global price shocks <\s>
<s> dominica the dominican economy has been dependent on agriculture primarily bananas in years past but increasingly has been driven by tourism as the government seeks to promote dominica as an ecotourism destination <\s>
<s> in order to diversify the island's production base the government also is attempting to develop an offshore financial sector and has signed an agreement with the eu to develop geothermal energy resources <\s>
<s> in 2003 the government began a comprehensive restructuring of the economy including elimination of price controls privatization of the state banana company and tax increases to address an economic and financial crisis and to meet imf requirements <\s>
<s> this restructuring paved the way for an economic recovery real growth for 2006 reached a two-decade high and helped to reduce the debt burden which remains at about 85 of gdp <\s>
<s> hurricane dean struck the island in august 2007 causing damages equivalent to 20 of gdp <\s>
<s> in 2009 growth slowed as a result of the global recession it picked up only slightly in 2010 <\s>
<s> dominican republic the dominican republic has long been viewed primarily as an exporter of sugar coffee and tobacco but in recent years the service sector has overtaken agriculture as the economy's largest employer due to growth in tourism and free trade zones <\s>
<s> the economy is highly dependent upon the us the destination for nearly 60 of exports <\s>
<s> remittances from the us amount to about a tenth of gdp equivalent to almost half of exports and three-quarters of tourism receipts <\s>
<s> the country suffers from marked income inequality the poorest half of the population receives less than one-fifth of gdp while the richest 10 enjoys nearly 40 of gdp <\s>
<s> high unemployment and underemployment remains an important long-term challenge <\s>
<s> the central america-dominican republic free trade agreement cafta-dr came into force in march 2007 boosting investment and exports and reducing losses to the asian garment industry <\s>
<s> the growth of the dominican republic's economy slowed in 2008-09 because of the global recession but still remained one of the fastest growing in the region <\s>
<s> ecuador ecuador is substantially dependent on its petroleum resources which have accounted for more than half of the country's export earnings and one-fourth of public sector revenues in recent years <\s>
<s> in 1999/2000 ecuador suffered a severe economic crisis with gdp contracting by more than 6 <\s>
<s> poverty increased significantly the banking system collapsed and ecuador defaulted on its external debt later that year <\s>
<s> in march 2000 the congress approved a series of structural reforms that also provided for the adoption of the us dollar as legal tender <\s>
<s> dollarization stabilized the economy and positive growth returned in the years that followed helped by high oil prices remittances and increased non-traditional exports <\s>
<s> from 2002-06 the economy grew 5.5 the highest five-year average in 25 years <\s>
<s> after moderate growth in 2007 the economy reached a growth rate of 7.2 in 2008 in large part due to high global petroleum prices <\s>
<s> president rafael correa who took office in january 2007 defaulted on ecuador's sovereign debt in december 2008 refusing to make payment on 3.2 billion in international bonds representing over 80 of ecuador's private external debt <\s>
<s> economic policies under the correa administration including an announcement in late 2009 terminating 13 bilateral investment treaties have generated economic uncertainty and discouraged private investment <\s>
<s> the ecuadorian economy slowed to 0.4 growth in 2009 due to the global financial crisis and the sharp decline in world oil prices and remittance flows but picked up to a 2.4 growth rate in 2010 <\s>

<s> eritrea since independence from ethiopia in 1993 eritrea has faced the economic problems of a small desperately poor country accentuated by the recent implementation of restrictive economic policies <\s>
<s> eritrea has a command economy under the control of the sole political party the people's front for democracy and justice pfdj <\s>
<s> like the economies of many african nations a large share of the population nearly 80 is engaged in subsistence agriculture but they produce only a small share of total output <\s>
<s> since the conclusion of the ethiopian-eritrea war in 2000 the government has maintained a firm grip on the economy expanding the use of the military and party-owned businesses to complete eritrea's development agenda <\s>
<s> the government strictly controls the use of foreign currency by limiting access and availability <\s>
<s> few private enterprises remain in eritrea <\s>
<s> eritrea's economy depends heavily on taxes paid by members of the diaspora <\s>
<s> erratic rainfall and the delayed demobilization of agriculturalists from the military continue to interfere with agricultural production and eritrea's recent harvests have been unable to meet the food needs of the country <\s>
<s> the government continues to place its hope for additional revenue on the development of several international mining projects <\s>
<s> despite difficulties for international companies in working with the eritrean government a canadian mining company signed a contract with the government in 2007 and began mineral extraction in 2010 <\s>
<s> eritrea's economic future depends upon its ability to master social problems such as illiteracy unemployment and low skills and more importantly on the government's willingness to support a true market economy <\s>
<s> nevertheless the economy in the area under government control has grown at a rate well above the eu average since 2000 <\s>
<s> cyprus joined the european exchange rate mechanism erm 2 in may 2005 and adopted the euro as its national currency on 1 january 2008 <\s>
<s> an aggressive austerity program in the preceding years aimed at paving the way for the euro helped turn a soaring fiscal deficit 6.3 in 2003 into a surplus of 1.2 in 2008 and reduced inflation to 4.7 <\s>
<s> this prosperity came under pressure in 2009 as construction and tourism slowed in the face of reduced foreign demand triggered by the ongoing global financial crisis <\s>
<s> although cyprus lagged its eu peers in showing signs of stress from the global crisis the economy tipped into recession in mid 2009 and contracted 1.8 for the year <\s>
<s> in addition the budget deficit is on the rise and reached 5.7 of gdp in 2010 a violation of the eu's budget deficit criteria of no more than 3 of gdp <\s>
<s> in response to the country's deteriorating finances nicosia is promising to implement measures to cut the cost of the state payroll curb tax evasion and revamp social benefits <\s>
<s> however it has been slow to act lacking a consensus in parliament and among the social partners for its proposed measures <\s>
<s> czech republic the czech republic is one of the most stable and prosperous of the post-communist states of central and eastern europe <\s>
<s> maintaining an open investment climate has been a key element of the czech republic's transition from a communist centrally planned economy to a functioning market economy <\s>
<s> as a member of the european union with an advantageous location in the center of europe a relatively low cost structure and a well-qualified labor force the czech republic is an attractive destination for foreign investment <\s>
<s> prior to its eu accession in 2004 the czech government harmonized its laws and regulations with those of the european union <\s>
<s> the small open export-driven czech economy grew by over 6 annually from 2005-2007 and by 2.5 in 2008 <\s>
<s> the conservative czech financial system has remained relatively healthy throughout 2009 <\s>
<s> nevertheless the real economy contracted by 4.1 in 2009 mainly due to a significant drop in external demand as the czech republic's main export markets fell into recession <\s>
<s> gdp is expected to grow by 2.4 in 2010 driven largely by a rebound in external demand particularly from gremany <\s>
<s> denmark this thoroughly modern market economy features a high-tech agricultural sector state-of-the-art industry with world-leading firms in pharmaceuticals maritime shipping and renewable energy and a high dependence on foreign trade <\s>
<s> the danish economy is also characterized by extensive government welfare measures an equitable distribution of income and comfortable living standards <\s>
<s> denmark is a net exporter of food and energy and enjoys a comfortable balance of payments surplus <\s>
<s> after a long consumption-driven upswing denmark's economy began slowing in 2007 with the end of a housing boom <\s>
<s> housing prices dropped markedly in 2008-09 <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis has exacerbated this cyclical slowdown through increased borrowing costs and lower export demand consumer confidence and investment <\s>
<s> the global financial crises cut danish gdp by 0.9 in 2008 and 4.7 in 2009 <\s>
<s> historically low levels of unemployment rose sharply with the recession but remain below 5 about half the level of the eu <\s>
<s> denmark made a modest recovery in 2010 in part because of increased government spending <\s>
<s> an impending decline in the ratio of workers to retirees will be a major long-term issue <\s>
<s> denmark maintained a healthy budget surplus for many years up to 2008 but the budget balance swung into deficit during 2009-10 <\s>
<s> nonetheless denmark's fiscal position remains among the strongest in the eu <\s>
<s> despite previously meeting the criteria to join the european economic and monetary union emu so far denmark has decided not to join although the danish krone remains pegged to the euro <\s>
<s> dhekelia economic activity is limited to providing services to the military and their families located in dhekelia <\s>
<s> all food and manufactured goods must be imported <\s>
<s> djibouti the economy is based on service activities connected with the country's strategic location and status as a free trade zone in the horn of africa <\s>
<s> two-thirds of djibouti's inhabitants live in the capital city the remainder are mostly nomadic herders <\s>
<s> scanty rainfall limits crop production to fruits and vegetables and most food must be imported <\s>
<s> djibouti provides services as both a transit port for the region and an international transshipment and refueling center <\s>
<s> imports and exports from landlocked neighbor ethiopia represent 70 of port activity at djibouti's container terminal <\s>
<s> djibouti has few natural resources and little industry <\s>
<s> the nation is therefore heavily dependent on foreign assistance to help support its balance of payments and to finance development projects <\s>
<s> an unemployment rate of nearly 60 in urban areas continues to be a major problem <\s>
<s> while inflation is not a concern due to the fixed tie of the djiboutian franc to the us dollar the artificially high value of the djiboutian franc adversely affects djibouti's balance of payments <\s>
<s> per capita consumption dropped an estimated 35 between 1999 and 2006 because of recession civil war and a high population growth rate including immigrants and refugees <\s>
<s> djibouti has experienced relatively minimal impact from the global economic downturn but its reliance on diesel-generated electricity and imported food leave average consumers vulnerable to global price shocks <\s>
<s> dominica the dominican economy has been dependent on agriculture primarily bananas in years past but increasingly has been driven by tourism as the government seeks to promote dominica as an ecotourism destination <\s>
<s> in order to diversify the island's production base the government also is attempting to develop an offshore financial sector and has signed an agreement with the eu to develop geothermal energy resources <\s>
<s> in 2003 the government began a comprehensive restructuring of the economy including elimination of price controls privatization of the state banana company and tax increases to address an economic and financial crisis and to meet imf requirements <\s>
<s> this restructuring paved the way for an economic recovery real growth for 2006 reached a two-decade high and helped to reduce the debt burden which remains at about 85 of gdp <\s>
<s> hurricane dean struck the island in august 2007 causing damages equivalent to 20 of gdp <\s>
<s> in 2009 growth slowed as a result of the global recession it picked up only slightly in 2010 <\s>
<s> dominican republic the dominican republic has long been viewed primarily as an exporter of sugar coffee and tobacco but in recent years the service sector has overtaken agriculture as the economy's largest employer due to growth in tourism and free trade zones <\s>
<s> the economy is highly dependent upon the us the destination for nearly 60 of exports <\s>
<s> remittances from the us amount to about a tenth of gdp equivalent to almost half of exports and three-quarters of tourism receipts <\s>
<s> the country suffers from marked income inequality the poorest half of the population receives less than one-fifth of gdp while the richest 10 enjoys nearly 40 of gdp <\s>
<s> high unemployment and underemployment remains an important long-term challenge <\s>
<s> the central america-dominican republic free trade agreement cafta-dr came into force in march 2007 boosting investment and exports and reducing losses to the asian garment industry <\s>
<s> the growth of the dominican republic's economy slowed in 2008-09 because of the global recession but still remained one of the fastest growing in the region <\s>
<s> ecuador ecuador is substantially dependent on its petroleum resources which have accounted for more than half of the country's export earnings and one-fourth of public sector revenues in recent years <\s>
<s> in 1999/2000 ecuador suffered a severe economic crisis with gdp contracting by more than 6 <\s>
<s> poverty increased significantly the banking system collapsed and ecuador defaulted on its external debt later that year <\s>
<s> in march 2000 the congress approved a series of structural reforms that also provided for the adoption of the us dollar as legal tender <\s>
<s> dollarization stabilized the economy and positive growth returned in the years that followed helped by high oil prices remittances and increased non-traditional exports <\s>
<s> from 2002-06 the economy grew 5.5 the highest five-year average in 25 years <\s>
<s> after moderate growth in 2007 the economy reached a growth rate of 7.2 in 2008 in large part due to high global petroleum prices <\s>
<s> president rafael correa who took office in january 2007 defaulted on ecuador's sovereign debt in december 2008 refusing to make payment on 3.2 billion in international bonds representing over 80 of ecuador's private external debt <\s>
<s> economic policies under the correa administration including an announcement in late 2009 terminating 13 bilateral investment treaties have generated economic uncertainty and discouraged private investment <\s>
<s> the ecuadorian economy slowed to 0.4 growth in 2009 due to the global financial crisis and the sharp decline in world oil prices and remittance flows but picked up to a 2.4 growth rate in 2010 <\s>
<s> egypt occupying the northeast corner of the african continent egypt is bisected by the highly fertile nile valley where most economic activity takes place <\s>
<s> egypt's economy was highly centralized during the rule of former president gamal abdel nasser but has opened up considerably under former president anwar el-sadat and current president mohamed hosni mubarak <\s>
<s> cairo from 2004 to 2008 aggressively pursued economic reforms to attract foreign investment and facilitate gdp growth <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis has slowed the reform efforts <\s>
<s> the budget deficit climbed to over 8 of gdp and egypt's gdp growth slowed to 4.6 in 2009 predominately due to reduced growth in export-oriented sectors including manufacturing and tourism and suez canal revenues <\s>
<s> in 2010 the government spent more on infrastructure and public projects and exports drove gdp growth to more than 5 but gdp growth in 2011 is unlikely to bounce back to pre-global financial recession levels when it stood at 7 <\s>
<s> despite the relatively high levels of economic growth over the past few years living conditions for the average egyptian remain poor <\s>
<s> el salvador despite being the smallest country geographically in central america el salvador has the third largest economy in the region <\s>
<s> the economy took a hit from the global recession and real gdp contracted by 3.5 in 2009 <\s>
<s> the economy began a slow recovery in 2010 on the back of improved export and remittances figures <\s>
<s> remittances accounted for 16 of gdp in 2009 and about a third of all households receive these transfers <\s>
<s> in 2006 el salvador was the first country to ratify the dominican republic-central american free trade agreement cafta-dr which has bolstered the export of processed foods sugar and ethanol and supported investment in the apparel sector amid increased asian competition and the expiration of the multi-fiber agreement in 2005 <\s>
<s> el salvador has promoted an open trade and investment environment and has embarked on a wave of privatizations extending to telecom electricity distribution banking and pension funds <\s>
<s> in late 2006 the government and the millennium challenge corporation signed a five-year 461 million compact to stimulate economic growth and reduce poverty in the country's northern region the primary conflict zone during the civil war through investments in education public services enterprise development and transportation infrastructure <\s>
<s> with the adoption of the us dollar as its currency in 2001 el salvador lost control over monetary policy <\s>
<s> any counter-cyclical policy response to the downturn must be through fiscal policy which is constrained by legislative requirements for a two-thirds majority to approve any international financing <\s>
<s> equatorial guinea the discovery and exploitation of large oil reserves have contributed to dramatic economic growth but fluctuating oil prices have produced huge swings in gdp growth in recent years <\s>
<s> forestry farming and fishing are also major components of gdp <\s>
<s> subsistence farming is the dominate form of livelihood <\s>
<s> although pre-independence equatorial guinea counted on cocoa production for hard currency earnings the neglect of the rural economy under successive regimes has diminished potential for agriculture-led growth the government has stated its intention to reinvest some oil revenue into agriculture <\s>
<s> a number of aid programs sponsored by the world bank and the imf have been cut off since 1993 because of corruption and mismanagement <\s>
<s> government officials and their family members own most businesses but corruption is rampant <\s>

<s> the small open export-driven czech economy grew by over 6 annually from 2005-2007 and by 2.5 in 2008 <\s>
<s> the conservative czech financial system has remained relatively healthy throughout 2009 <\s>
<s> nevertheless the real economy contracted by 4.1 in 2009 mainly due to a significant drop in external demand as the czech republic's main export markets fell into recession <\s>
<s> gdp is expected to grow by 2.4 in 2010 driven largely by a rebound in external demand particularly from gremany <\s>
<s> denmark this thoroughly modern market economy features a high-tech agricultural sector state-of-the-art industry with world-leading firms in pharmaceuticals maritime shipping and renewable energy and a high dependence on foreign trade <\s>
<s> the danish economy is also characterized by extensive government welfare measures an equitable distribution of income and comfortable living standards <\s>
<s> denmark is a net exporter of food and energy and enjoys a comfortable balance of payments surplus <\s>
<s> after a long consumption-driven upswing denmark's economy began slowing in 2007 with the end of a housing boom <\s>
<s> housing prices dropped markedly in 2008-09 <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis has exacerbated this cyclical slowdown through increased borrowing costs and lower export demand consumer confidence and investment <\s>
<s> the global financial crises cut danish gdp by 0.9 in 2008 and 4.7 in 2009 <\s>
<s> historically low levels of unemployment rose sharply with the recession but remain below 5 about half the level of the eu <\s>
<s> denmark made a modest recovery in 2010 in part because of increased government spending <\s>
<s> an impending decline in the ratio of workers to retirees will be a major long-term issue <\s>
<s> denmark maintained a healthy budget surplus for many years up to 2008 but the budget balance swung into deficit during 2009-10 <\s>
<s> nonetheless denmark's fiscal position remains among the strongest in the eu <\s>
<s> despite previously meeting the criteria to join the european economic and monetary union emu so far denmark has decided not to join although the danish krone remains pegged to the euro <\s>
<s> dhekelia economic activity is limited to providing services to the military and their families located in dhekelia <\s>
<s> all food and manufactured goods must be imported <\s>
<s> djibouti the economy is based on service activities connected with the country's strategic location and status as a free trade zone in the horn of africa <\s>
<s> two-thirds of djibouti's inhabitants live in the capital city the remainder are mostly nomadic herders <\s>
<s> scanty rainfall limits crop production to fruits and vegetables and most food must be imported <\s>
<s> djibouti provides services as both a transit port for the region and an international transshipment and refueling center <\s>
<s> imports and exports from landlocked neighbor ethiopia represent 70 of port activity at djibouti's container terminal <\s>
<s> djibouti has few natural resources and little industry <\s>
<s> the nation is therefore heavily dependent on foreign assistance to help support its balance of payments and to finance development projects <\s>
<s> an unemployment rate of nearly 60 in urban areas continues to be a major problem <\s>
<s> while inflation is not a concern due to the fixed tie of the djiboutian franc to the us dollar the artificially high value of the djiboutian franc adversely affects djibouti's balance of payments <\s>
<s> per capita consumption dropped an estimated 35 between 1999 and 2006 because of recession civil war and a high population growth rate including immigrants and refugees <\s>
<s> djibouti has experienced relatively minimal impact from the global economic downturn but its reliance on diesel-generated electricity and imported food leave average consumers vulnerable to global price shocks <\s>
<s> dominica the dominican economy has been dependent on agriculture primarily bananas in years past but increasingly has been driven by tourism as the government seeks to promote dominica as an ecotourism destination <\s>
<s> in order to diversify the island's production base the government also is attempting to develop an offshore financial sector and has signed an agreement with the eu to develop geothermal energy resources <\s>
<s> in 2003 the government began a comprehensive restructuring of the economy including elimination of price controls privatization of the state banana company and tax increases to address an economic and financial crisis and to meet imf requirements <\s>
<s> this restructuring paved the way for an economic recovery real growth for 2006 reached a two-decade high and helped to reduce the debt burden which remains at about 85 of gdp <\s>
<s> hurricane dean struck the island in august 2007 causing damages equivalent to 20 of gdp <\s>
<s> in 2009 growth slowed as a result of the global recession it picked up only slightly in 2010 <\s>
<s> dominican republic the dominican republic has long been viewed primarily as an exporter of sugar coffee and tobacco but in recent years the service sector has overtaken agriculture as the economy's largest employer due to growth in tourism and free trade zones <\s>
<s> the economy is highly dependent upon the us the destination for nearly 60 of exports <\s>
<s> remittances from the us amount to about a tenth of gdp equivalent to almost half of exports and three-quarters of tourism receipts <\s>
<s> the country suffers from marked income inequality the poorest half of the population receives less than one-fifth of gdp while the richest 10 enjoys nearly 40 of gdp <\s>
<s> high unemployment and underemployment remains an important long-term challenge <\s>
<s> the central america-dominican republic free trade agreement cafta-dr came into force in march 2007 boosting investment and exports and reducing losses to the asian garment industry <\s>
<s> the growth of the dominican republic's economy slowed in 2008-09 because of the global recession but still remained one of the fastest growing in the region <\s>
<s> ecuador ecuador is substantially dependent on its petroleum resources which have accounted for more than half of the country's export earnings and one-fourth of public sector revenues in recent years <\s>
<s> in 1999/2000 ecuador suffered a severe economic crisis with gdp contracting by more than 6 <\s>
<s> poverty increased significantly the banking system collapsed and ecuador defaulted on its external debt later that year <\s>
<s> in march 2000 the congress approved a series of structural reforms that also provided for the adoption of the us dollar as legal tender <\s>
<s> dollarization stabilized the economy and positive growth returned in the years that followed helped by high oil prices remittances and increased non-traditional exports <\s>
<s> from 2002-06 the economy grew 5.5 the highest five-year average in 25 years <\s>
<s> after moderate growth in 2007 the economy reached a growth rate of 7.2 in 2008 in large part due to high global petroleum prices <\s>
<s> president rafael correa who took office in january 2007 defaulted on ecuador's sovereign debt in december 2008 refusing to make payment on 3.2 billion in international bonds representing over 80 of ecuador's private external debt <\s>
<s> economic policies under the correa administration including an announcement in late 2009 terminating 13 bilateral investment treaties have generated economic uncertainty and discouraged private investment <\s>
<s> the ecuadorian economy slowed to 0.4 growth in 2009 due to the global financial crisis and the sharp decline in world oil prices and remittance flows but picked up to a 2.4 growth rate in 2010 <\s>
<s> egypt occupying the northeast corner of the african continent egypt is bisected by the highly fertile nile valley where most economic activity takes place <\s>
<s> egypt's economy was highly centralized during the rule of former president gamal abdel nasser but has opened up considerably under former president anwar el-sadat and current president mohamed hosni mubarak <\s>
<s> cairo from 2004 to 2008 aggressively pursued economic reforms to attract foreign investment and facilitate gdp growth <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis has slowed the reform efforts <\s>
<s> the budget deficit climbed to over 8 of gdp and egypt's gdp growth slowed to 4.6 in 2009 predominately due to reduced growth in export-oriented sectors including manufacturing and tourism and suez canal revenues <\s>
<s> in 2010 the government spent more on infrastructure and public projects and exports drove gdp growth to more than 5 but gdp growth in 2011 is unlikely to bounce back to pre-global financial recession levels when it stood at 7 <\s>
<s> despite the relatively high levels of economic growth over the past few years living conditions for the average egyptian remain poor <\s>
<s> el salvador despite being the smallest country geographically in central america el salvador has the third largest economy in the region <\s>
<s> the economy took a hit from the global recession and real gdp contracted by 3.5 in 2009 <\s>
<s> the economy began a slow recovery in 2010 on the back of improved export and remittances figures <\s>
<s> remittances accounted for 16 of gdp in 2009 and about a third of all households receive these transfers <\s>
<s> in 2006 el salvador was the first country to ratify the dominican republic-central american free trade agreement cafta-dr which has bolstered the export of processed foods sugar and ethanol and supported investment in the apparel sector amid increased asian competition and the expiration of the multi-fiber agreement in 2005 <\s>
<s> el salvador has promoted an open trade and investment environment and has embarked on a wave of privatizations extending to telecom electricity distribution banking and pension funds <\s>
<s> in late 2006 the government and the millennium challenge corporation signed a five-year 461 million compact to stimulate economic growth and reduce poverty in the country's northern region the primary conflict zone during the civil war through investments in education public services enterprise development and transportation infrastructure <\s>
<s> with the adoption of the us dollar as its currency in 2001 el salvador lost control over monetary policy <\s>
<s> any counter-cyclical policy response to the downturn must be through fiscal policy which is constrained by legislative requirements for a two-thirds majority to approve any international financing <\s>
<s> equatorial guinea the discovery and exploitation of large oil reserves have contributed to dramatic economic growth but fluctuating oil prices have produced huge swings in gdp growth in recent years <\s>
<s> forestry farming and fishing are also major components of gdp <\s>
<s> subsistence farming is the dominate form of livelihood <\s>
<s> although pre-independence equatorial guinea counted on cocoa production for hard currency earnings the neglect of the rural economy under successive regimes has diminished potential for agriculture-led growth the government has stated its intention to reinvest some oil revenue into agriculture <\s>
<s> a number of aid programs sponsored by the world bank and the imf have been cut off since 1993 because of corruption and mismanagement <\s>
<s> government officials and their family members own most businesses but corruption is rampant <\s>
<s> undeveloped natural resources include titanium iron ore manganese uranium and alluvial gold <\s>
<s> growth remained strong in 2008 led by oil but dropped in 2009-10 as the price of oil fell <\s>
<s> eritrea since independence from ethiopia in 1993 eritrea has faced the economic problems of a small desperately poor country accentuated by the recent implementation of restrictive economic policies <\s>
<s> eritrea has a command economy under the control of the sole political party the people's front for democracy and justice pfdj <\s>
<s> like the economies of many african nations a large share of the population nearly 80 is engaged in subsistence agriculture but they produce only a small share of total output <\s>
<s> since the conclusion of the ethiopian-eritrea war in 2000 the government has maintained a firm grip on the economy expanding the use of the military and party-owned businesses to complete eritrea's development agenda <\s>
<s> the government strictly controls the use of foreign currency by limiting access and availability <\s>
<s> few private enterprises remain in eritrea <\s>
<s> eritrea's economy depends heavily on taxes paid by members of the diaspora <\s>
<s> erratic rainfall and the delayed demobilization of agriculturalists from the military continue to interfere with agricultural production and eritrea's recent harvests have been unable to meet the food needs of the country <\s>
<s> the government continues to place its hope for additional revenue on the development of several international mining projects <\s>
<s> despite difficulties for international companies in working with the eritrean government a canadian mining company signed a contract with the government in 2007 and began mineral extraction in 2010 <\s>
<s> eritrea's economic future depends upon its ability to master social problems such as illiteracy unemployment and low skills and more importantly on the government's willingness to support a true market economy <\s>
<s> nevertheless the economy in the area under government control has grown at a rate well above the eu average since 2000 <\s>
<s> cyprus joined the european exchange rate mechanism erm 2 in may 2005 and adopted the euro as its national currency on 1 january 2008 <\s>
<s> an aggressive austerity program in the preceding years aimed at paving the way for the euro helped turn a soaring fiscal deficit 6.3 in 2003 into a surplus of 1.2 in 2008 and reduced inflation to 4.7 <\s>
<s> this prosperity came under pressure in 2009 as construction and tourism slowed in the face of reduced foreign demand triggered by the ongoing global financial crisis <\s>
<s> although cyprus lagged its eu peers in showing signs of stress from the global crisis the economy tipped into recession in mid 2009 and contracted 1.8 for the year <\s>
<s> in addition the budget deficit is on the rise and reached 5.7 of gdp in 2010 a violation of the eu's budget deficit criteria of no more than 3 of gdp <\s>
<s> in response to the country's deteriorating finances nicosia is promising to implement measures to cut the cost of the state payroll curb tax evasion and revamp social benefits <\s>
<s> however it has been slow to act lacking a consensus in parliament and among the social partners for its proposed measures <\s>
<s> czech republic the czech republic is one of the most stable and prosperous of the post-communist states of central and eastern europe <\s>
<s> maintaining an open investment climate has been a key element of the czech republic's transition from a communist centrally planned economy to a functioning market economy <\s>

<s> per capita consumption dropped an estimated 35 between 1999 and 2006 because of recession civil war and a high population growth rate including immigrants and refugees <\s>
<s> djibouti has experienced relatively minimal impact from the global economic downturn but its reliance on diesel-generated electricity and imported food leave average consumers vulnerable to global price shocks <\s>
<s> dominica the dominican economy has been dependent on agriculture primarily bananas in years past but increasingly has been driven by tourism as the government seeks to promote dominica as an ecotourism destination <\s>
<s> in order to diversify the island's production base the government also is attempting to develop an offshore financial sector and has signed an agreement with the eu to develop geothermal energy resources <\s>
<s> in 2003 the government began a comprehensive restructuring of the economy including elimination of price controls privatization of the state banana company and tax increases to address an economic and financial crisis and to meet imf requirements <\s>
<s> this restructuring paved the way for an economic recovery real growth for 2006 reached a two-decade high and helped to reduce the debt burden which remains at about 85 of gdp <\s>
<s> hurricane dean struck the island in august 2007 causing damages equivalent to 20 of gdp <\s>
<s> in 2009 growth slowed as a result of the global recession it picked up only slightly in 2010 <\s>
<s> dominican republic the dominican republic has long been viewed primarily as an exporter of sugar coffee and tobacco but in recent years the service sector has overtaken agriculture as the economy's largest employer due to growth in tourism and free trade zones <\s>
<s> the economy is highly dependent upon the us the destination for nearly 60 of exports <\s>
<s> remittances from the us amount to about a tenth of gdp equivalent to almost half of exports and three-quarters of tourism receipts <\s>
<s> the country suffers from marked income inequality the poorest half of the population receives less than one-fifth of gdp while the richest 10 enjoys nearly 40 of gdp <\s>
<s> high unemployment and underemployment remains an important long-term challenge <\s>
<s> the central america-dominican republic free trade agreement cafta-dr came into force in march 2007 boosting investment and exports and reducing losses to the asian garment industry <\s>
<s> the growth of the dominican republic's economy slowed in 2008-09 because of the global recession but still remained one of the fastest growing in the region <\s>
<s> ecuador ecuador is substantially dependent on its petroleum resources which have accounted for more than half of the country's export earnings and one-fourth of public sector revenues in recent years <\s>
<s> in 1999/2000 ecuador suffered a severe economic crisis with gdp contracting by more than 6 <\s>
<s> poverty increased significantly the banking system collapsed and ecuador defaulted on its external debt later that year <\s>
<s> in march 2000 the congress approved a series of structural reforms that also provided for the adoption of the us dollar as legal tender <\s>
<s> dollarization stabilized the economy and positive growth returned in the years that followed helped by high oil prices remittances and increased non-traditional exports <\s>
<s> from 2002-06 the economy grew 5.5 the highest five-year average in 25 years <\s>
<s> after moderate growth in 2007 the economy reached a growth rate of 7.2 in 2008 in large part due to high global petroleum prices <\s>
<s> president rafael correa who took office in january 2007 defaulted on ecuador's sovereign debt in december 2008 refusing to make payment on 3.2 billion in international bonds representing over 80 of ecuador's private external debt <\s>
<s> economic policies under the correa administration including an announcement in late 2009 terminating 13 bilateral investment treaties have generated economic uncertainty and discouraged private investment <\s>
<s> the ecuadorian economy slowed to 0.4 growth in 2009 due to the global financial crisis and the sharp decline in world oil prices and remittance flows but picked up to a 2.4 growth rate in 2010 <\s>
<s> egypt occupying the northeast corner of the african continent egypt is bisected by the highly fertile nile valley where most economic activity takes place <\s>
<s> egypt's economy was highly centralized during the rule of former president gamal abdel nasser but has opened up considerably under former president anwar el-sadat and current president mohamed hosni mubarak <\s>
<s> cairo from 2004 to 2008 aggressively pursued economic reforms to attract foreign investment and facilitate gdp growth <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis has slowed the reform efforts <\s>
<s> the budget deficit climbed to over 8 of gdp and egypt's gdp growth slowed to 4.6 in 2009 predominately due to reduced growth in export-oriented sectors including manufacturing and tourism and suez canal revenues <\s>
<s> in 2010 the government spent more on infrastructure and public projects and exports drove gdp growth to more than 5 but gdp growth in 2011 is unlikely to bounce back to pre-global financial recession levels when it stood at 7 <\s>
<s> despite the relatively high levels of economic growth over the past few years living conditions for the average egyptian remain poor <\s>
<s> el salvador despite being the smallest country geographically in central america el salvador has the third largest economy in the region <\s>
<s> the economy took a hit from the global recession and real gdp contracted by 3.5 in 2009 <\s>
<s> the economy began a slow recovery in 2010 on the back of improved export and remittances figures <\s>
<s> remittances accounted for 16 of gdp in 2009 and about a third of all households receive these transfers <\s>
<s> in 2006 el salvador was the first country to ratify the dominican republic-central american free trade agreement cafta-dr which has bolstered the export of processed foods sugar and ethanol and supported investment in the apparel sector amid increased asian competition and the expiration of the multi-fiber agreement in 2005 <\s>
<s> el salvador has promoted an open trade and investment environment and has embarked on a wave of privatizations extending to telecom electricity distribution banking and pension funds <\s>
<s> in late 2006 the government and the millennium challenge corporation signed a five-year 461 million compact to stimulate economic growth and reduce poverty in the country's northern region the primary conflict zone during the civil war through investments in education public services enterprise development and transportation infrastructure <\s>
<s> with the adoption of the us dollar as its currency in 2001 el salvador lost control over monetary policy <\s>
<s> any counter-cyclical policy response to the downturn must be through fiscal policy which is constrained by legislative requirements for a two-thirds majority to approve any international financing <\s>
<s> equatorial guinea the discovery and exploitation of large oil reserves have contributed to dramatic economic growth but fluctuating oil prices have produced huge swings in gdp growth in recent years <\s>
<s> forestry farming and fishing are also major components of gdp <\s>
<s> subsistence farming is the dominate form of livelihood <\s>
<s> although pre-independence equatorial guinea counted on cocoa production for hard currency earnings the neglect of the rural economy under successive regimes has diminished potential for agriculture-led growth the government has stated its intention to reinvest some oil revenue into agriculture <\s>
<s> a number of aid programs sponsored by the world bank and the imf have been cut off since 1993 because of corruption and mismanagement <\s>
<s> government officials and their family members own most businesses but corruption is rampant <\s>
<s> undeveloped natural resources include titanium iron ore manganese uranium and alluvial gold <\s>
<s> growth remained strong in 2008 led by oil but dropped in 2009-10 as the price of oil fell <\s>
<s> eritrea since independence from ethiopia in 1993 eritrea has faced the economic problems of a small desperately poor country accentuated by the recent implementation of restrictive economic policies <\s>
<s> eritrea has a command economy under the control of the sole political party the people's front for democracy and justice pfdj <\s>
<s> like the economies of many african nations a large share of the population nearly 80 is engaged in subsistence agriculture but they produce only a small share of total output <\s>
<s> since the conclusion of the ethiopian-eritrea war in 2000 the government has maintained a firm grip on the economy expanding the use of the military and party-owned businesses to complete eritrea's development agenda <\s>
<s> the government strictly controls the use of foreign currency by limiting access and availability <\s>
<s> few private enterprises remain in eritrea <\s>
<s> eritrea's economy depends heavily on taxes paid by members of the diaspora <\s>
<s> erratic rainfall and the delayed demobilization of agriculturalists from the military continue to interfere with agricultural production and eritrea's recent harvests have been unable to meet the food needs of the country <\s>
<s> the government continues to place its hope for additional revenue on the development of several international mining projects <\s>
<s> despite difficulties for international companies in working with the eritrean government a canadian mining company signed a contract with the government in 2007 and began mineral extraction in 2010 <\s>
<s> eritrea's economic future depends upon its ability to master social problems such as illiteracy unemployment and low skills and more importantly on the government's willingness to support a true market economy <\s>
<s> nevertheless the economy in the area under government control has grown at a rate well above the eu average since 2000 <\s>
<s> cyprus joined the european exchange rate mechanism erm 2 in may 2005 and adopted the euro as its national currency on 1 january 2008 <\s>
<s> an aggressive austerity program in the preceding years aimed at paving the way for the euro helped turn a soaring fiscal deficit 6.3 in 2003 into a surplus of 1.2 in 2008 and reduced inflation to 4.7 <\s>
<s> this prosperity came under pressure in 2009 as construction and tourism slowed in the face of reduced foreign demand triggered by the ongoing global financial crisis <\s>
<s> although cyprus lagged its eu peers in showing signs of stress from the global crisis the economy tipped into recession in mid 2009 and contracted 1.8 for the year <\s>
<s> in addition the budget deficit is on the rise and reached 5.7 of gdp in 2010 a violation of the eu's budget deficit criteria of no more than 3 of gdp <\s>
<s> in response to the country's deteriorating finances nicosia is promising to implement measures to cut the cost of the state payroll curb tax evasion and revamp social benefits <\s>
<s> however it has been slow to act lacking a consensus in parliament and among the social partners for its proposed measures <\s>
<s> czech republic the czech republic is one of the most stable and prosperous of the post-communist states of central and eastern europe <\s>
<s> maintaining an open investment climate has been a key element of the czech republic's transition from a communist centrally planned economy to a functioning market economy <\s>
<s> as a member of the european union with an advantageous location in the center of europe a relatively low cost structure and a well-qualified labor force the czech republic is an attractive destination for foreign investment <\s>
<s> prior to its eu accession in 2004 the czech government harmonized its laws and regulations with those of the european union <\s>
<s> the small open export-driven czech economy grew by over 6 annually from 2005-2007 and by 2.5 in 2008 <\s>
<s> the conservative czech financial system has remained relatively healthy throughout 2009 <\s>
<s> nevertheless the real economy contracted by 4.1 in 2009 mainly due to a significant drop in external demand as the czech republic's main export markets fell into recession <\s>
<s> gdp is expected to grow by 2.4 in 2010 driven largely by a rebound in external demand particularly from gremany <\s>
<s> denmark this thoroughly modern market economy features a high-tech agricultural sector state-of-the-art industry with world-leading firms in pharmaceuticals maritime shipping and renewable energy and a high dependence on foreign trade <\s>
<s> the danish economy is also characterized by extensive government welfare measures an equitable distribution of income and comfortable living standards <\s>
<s> denmark is a net exporter of food and energy and enjoys a comfortable balance of payments surplus <\s>
<s> after a long consumption-driven upswing denmark's economy began slowing in 2007 with the end of a housing boom <\s>
<s> housing prices dropped markedly in 2008-09 <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis has exacerbated this cyclical slowdown through increased borrowing costs and lower export demand consumer confidence and investment <\s>
<s> the global financial crises cut danish gdp by 0.9 in 2008 and 4.7 in 2009 <\s>
<s> historically low levels of unemployment rose sharply with the recession but remain below 5 about half the level of the eu <\s>
<s> denmark made a modest recovery in 2010 in part because of increased government spending <\s>
<s> an impending decline in the ratio of workers to retirees will be a major long-term issue <\s>
<s> denmark maintained a healthy budget surplus for many years up to 2008 but the budget balance swung into deficit during 2009-10 <\s>
<s> nonetheless denmark's fiscal position remains among the strongest in the eu <\s>
<s> despite previously meeting the criteria to join the european economic and monetary union emu so far denmark has decided not to join although the danish krone remains pegged to the euro <\s>
<s> dhekelia economic activity is limited to providing services to the military and their families located in dhekelia <\s>
<s> all food and manufactured goods must be imported <\s>
<s> djibouti the economy is based on service activities connected with the country's strategic location and status as a free trade zone in the horn of africa <\s>
<s> two-thirds of djibouti's inhabitants live in the capital city the remainder are mostly nomadic herders <\s>
<s> scanty rainfall limits crop production to fruits and vegetables and most food must be imported <\s>
<s> djibouti provides services as both a transit port for the region and an international transshipment and refueling center <\s>
<s> imports and exports from landlocked neighbor ethiopia represent 70 of port activity at djibouti's container terminal <\s>
<s> djibouti has few natural resources and little industry <\s>
<s> the nation is therefore heavily dependent on foreign assistance to help support its balance of payments and to finance development projects <\s>

<s> economic policies under the correa administration including an announcement in late 2009 terminating 13 bilateral investment treaties have generated economic uncertainty and discouraged private investment <\s>
<s> the ecuadorian economy slowed to 0.4 growth in 2009 due to the global financial crisis and the sharp decline in world oil prices and remittance flows but picked up to a 2.4 growth rate in 2010 <\s>
<s> egypt occupying the northeast corner of the african continent egypt is bisected by the highly fertile nile valley where most economic activity takes place <\s>
<s> egypt's economy was highly centralized during the rule of former president gamal abdel nasser but has opened up considerably under former president anwar el-sadat and current president mohamed hosni mubarak <\s>
<s> cairo from 2004 to 2008 aggressively pursued economic reforms to attract foreign investment and facilitate gdp growth <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis has slowed the reform efforts <\s>
<s> the budget deficit climbed to over 8 of gdp and egypt's gdp growth slowed to 4.6 in 2009 predominately due to reduced growth in export-oriented sectors including manufacturing and tourism and suez canal revenues <\s>
<s> in 2010 the government spent more on infrastructure and public projects and exports drove gdp growth to more than 5 but gdp growth in 2011 is unlikely to bounce back to pre-global financial recession levels when it stood at 7 <\s>
<s> despite the relatively high levels of economic growth over the past few years living conditions for the average egyptian remain poor <\s>
<s> el salvador despite being the smallest country geographically in central america el salvador has the third largest economy in the region <\s>
<s> the economy took a hit from the global recession and real gdp contracted by 3.5 in 2009 <\s>
<s> the economy began a slow recovery in 2010 on the back of improved export and remittances figures <\s>
<s> remittances accounted for 16 of gdp in 2009 and about a third of all households receive these transfers <\s>
<s> in 2006 el salvador was the first country to ratify the dominican republic-central american free trade agreement cafta-dr which has bolstered the export of processed foods sugar and ethanol and supported investment in the apparel sector amid increased asian competition and the expiration of the multi-fiber agreement in 2005 <\s>
<s> el salvador has promoted an open trade and investment environment and has embarked on a wave of privatizations extending to telecom electricity distribution banking and pension funds <\s>
<s> in late 2006 the government and the millennium challenge corporation signed a five-year 461 million compact to stimulate economic growth and reduce poverty in the country's northern region the primary conflict zone during the civil war through investments in education public services enterprise development and transportation infrastructure <\s>
<s> with the adoption of the us dollar as its currency in 2001 el salvador lost control over monetary policy <\s>
<s> any counter-cyclical policy response to the downturn must be through fiscal policy which is constrained by legislative requirements for a two-thirds majority to approve any international financing <\s>
<s> equatorial guinea the discovery and exploitation of large oil reserves have contributed to dramatic economic growth but fluctuating oil prices have produced huge swings in gdp growth in recent years <\s>
<s> forestry farming and fishing are also major components of gdp <\s>
<s> subsistence farming is the dominate form of livelihood <\s>
<s> although pre-independence equatorial guinea counted on cocoa production for hard currency earnings the neglect of the rural economy under successive regimes has diminished potential for agriculture-led growth the government has stated its intention to reinvest some oil revenue into agriculture <\s>
<s> a number of aid programs sponsored by the world bank and the imf have been cut off since 1993 because of corruption and mismanagement <\s>
<s> government officials and their family members own most businesses but corruption is rampant <\s>
<s> undeveloped natural resources include titanium iron ore manganese uranium and alluvial gold <\s>
<s> growth remained strong in 2008 led by oil but dropped in 2009-10 as the price of oil fell <\s>
<s> eritrea since independence from ethiopia in 1993 eritrea has faced the economic problems of a small desperately poor country accentuated by the recent implementation of restrictive economic policies <\s>
<s> eritrea has a command economy under the control of the sole political party the people's front for democracy and justice pfdj <\s>
<s> like the economies of many african nations a large share of the population nearly 80 is engaged in subsistence agriculture but they produce only a small share of total output <\s>
<s> since the conclusion of the ethiopian-eritrea war in 2000 the government has maintained a firm grip on the economy expanding the use of the military and party-owned businesses to complete eritrea's development agenda <\s>
<s> the government strictly controls the use of foreign currency by limiting access and availability <\s>
<s> few private enterprises remain in eritrea <\s>
<s> eritrea's economy depends heavily on taxes paid by members of the diaspora <\s>
<s> erratic rainfall and the delayed demobilization of agriculturalists from the military continue to interfere with agricultural production and eritrea's recent harvests have been unable to meet the food needs of the country <\s>
<s> the government continues to place its hope for additional revenue on the development of several international mining projects <\s>
<s> despite difficulties for international companies in working with the eritrean government a canadian mining company signed a contract with the government in 2007 and began mineral extraction in 2010 <\s>
<s> eritrea's economic future depends upon its ability to master social problems such as illiteracy unemployment and low skills and more importantly on the government's willingness to support a true market economy <\s>
<s> nevertheless the economy in the area under government control has grown at a rate well above the eu average since 2000 <\s>
<s> cyprus joined the european exchange rate mechanism erm 2 in may 2005 and adopted the euro as its national currency on 1 january 2008 <\s>
<s> an aggressive austerity program in the preceding years aimed at paving the way for the euro helped turn a soaring fiscal deficit 6.3 in 2003 into a surplus of 1.2 in 2008 and reduced inflation to 4.7 <\s>
<s> this prosperity came under pressure in 2009 as construction and tourism slowed in the face of reduced foreign demand triggered by the ongoing global financial crisis <\s>
<s> although cyprus lagged its eu peers in showing signs of stress from the global crisis the economy tipped into recession in mid 2009 and contracted 1.8 for the year <\s>
<s> in addition the budget deficit is on the rise and reached 5.7 of gdp in 2010 a violation of the eu's budget deficit criteria of no more than 3 of gdp <\s>
<s> in response to the country's deteriorating finances nicosia is promising to implement measures to cut the cost of the state payroll curb tax evasion and revamp social benefits <\s>
<s> however it has been slow to act lacking a consensus in parliament and among the social partners for its proposed measures <\s>
<s> czech republic the czech republic is one of the most stable and prosperous of the post-communist states of central and eastern europe <\s>
<s> maintaining an open investment climate has been a key element of the czech republic's transition from a communist centrally planned economy to a functioning market economy <\s>
<s> as a member of the european union with an advantageous location in the center of europe a relatively low cost structure and a well-qualified labor force the czech republic is an attractive destination for foreign investment <\s>
<s> prior to its eu accession in 2004 the czech government harmonized its laws and regulations with those of the european union <\s>
<s> the small open export-driven czech economy grew by over 6 annually from 2005-2007 and by 2.5 in 2008 <\s>
<s> the conservative czech financial system has remained relatively healthy throughout 2009 <\s>
<s> nevertheless the real economy contracted by 4.1 in 2009 mainly due to a significant drop in external demand as the czech republic's main export markets fell into recession <\s>
<s> gdp is expected to grow by 2.4 in 2010 driven largely by a rebound in external demand particularly from gremany <\s>
<s> denmark this thoroughly modern market economy features a high-tech agricultural sector state-of-the-art industry with world-leading firms in pharmaceuticals maritime shipping and renewable energy and a high dependence on foreign trade <\s>
<s> the danish economy is also characterized by extensive government welfare measures an equitable distribution of income and comfortable living standards <\s>
<s> denmark is a net exporter of food and energy and enjoys a comfortable balance of payments surplus <\s>
<s> after a long consumption-driven upswing denmark's economy began slowing in 2007 with the end of a housing boom <\s>
<s> housing prices dropped markedly in 2008-09 <\s>
<s> the global financial crisis has exacerbated this cyclical slowdown through increased borrowing costs and lower export demand consumer confidence and investment <\s>
<s> the global financial crises cut danish gdp by 0.9 in 2008 and 4.7 in 2009 <\s>
<s> historically low levels of unemployment rose sharply with the recession but remain below 5 about half the level of the eu <\s>
<s> denmark made a modest recovery in 2010 in part because of increased government spending <\s>
<s> an impending decline in the ratio of workers to retirees will be a major long-term issue <\s>
<s> denmark maintained a healthy budget surplus for many years up to 2008 but the budget balance swung into deficit during 2009-10 <\s>
<s> nonetheless denmark's fiscal position remains among the strongest in the eu <\s>
<s> despite previously meeting the criteria to join the european economic and monetary union emu so far denmark has decided not to join although the danish krone remains pegged to the euro <\s>
<s> dhekelia economic activity is limited to providing services to the military and their families located in dhekelia <\s>
<s> all food and manufactured goods must be imported <\s>
<s> djibouti the economy is based on service activities connected with the country's strategic location and status as a free trade zone in the horn of africa <\s>
<s> two-thirds of djibouti's inhabitants live in the capital city the remainder are mostly nomadic herders <\s>
<s> scanty rainfall limits crop production to fruits and vegetables and most food must be imported <\s>
<s> djibouti provides services as both a transit port for the region and an international transshipment and refueling center <\s>
<s> imports and exports from landlocked neighbor ethiopia represent 70 of port activity at djibouti's container terminal <\s>
<s> djibouti has few natural resources and little industry <\s>
<s> the nation is therefore heavily dependent on foreign assistance to help support its balance of payments and to finance development projects <\s>
<s> an unemployment rate of nearly 60 in urban areas continues to be a major problem <\s>
<s> while inflation is not a concern due to the fixed tie of the djiboutian franc to the us dollar the artificially high value of the djiboutian franc adversely affects djibouti's balance of payments <\s>
<s> per capita consumption dropped an estimated 35 between 1999 and 2006 because of recession civil war and a high population growth rate including immigrants and refugees <\s>
<s> djibouti has experienced relatively minimal impact from the global economic downturn but its reliance on diesel-generated electricity and imported food leave average consumers vulnerable to global price shocks <\s>
<s> dominica the dominican economy has been dependent on agriculture primarily bananas in years past but increasingly has been driven by tourism as the government seeks to promote dominica as an ecotourism destination <\s>
<s> in order to diversify the island's production base the government also is attempting to develop an offshore financial sector and has signed an agreement with the eu to develop geothermal energy resources <\s>
<s> in 2003 the government began a comprehensive restructuring of the economy including elimination of price controls privatization of the state banana company and tax increases to address an economic and financial crisis and to meet imf requirements <\s>
<s> this restructuring paved the way for an economic recovery real growth for 2006 reached a two-decade high and helped to reduce the debt burden which remains at about 85 of gdp <\s>
<s> hurricane dean struck the island in august 2007 causing damages equivalent to 20 of gdp <\s>
<s> in 2009 growth slowed as a result of the global recession it picked up only slightly in 2010 <\s>
<s> dominican republic the dominican republic has long been viewed primarily as an exporter of sugar coffee and tobacco but in recent years the service sector has overtaken agriculture as the economy's largest employer due to growth in tourism and free trade zones <\s>
<s> the economy is highly dependent upon the us the destination for nearly 60 of exports <\s>
<s> remittances from the us amount to about a tenth of gdp equivalent to almost half of exports and three-quarters of tourism receipts <\s>
<s> the country suffers from marked income inequality the poorest half of the population receives less than one-fifth of gdp while the richest 10 enjoys nearly 40 of gdp <\s>
<s> high unemployment and underemployment remains an important long-term challenge <\s>
<s> the central america-dominican republic free trade agreement cafta-dr came into force in march 2007 boosting investment and exports and reducing losses to the asian garment industry <\s>
<s> the growth of the dominican republic's economy slowed in 2008-09 because of the global recession but still remained one of the fastest growing in the region <\s>
<s> ecuador ecuador is substantially dependent on its petroleum resources which have accounted for more than half of the country's export earnings and one-fourth of public sector revenues in recent years <\s>
<s> in 1999/2000 ecuador suffered a severe economic crisis with gdp contracting by more than 6 <\s>
<s> poverty increased significantly the banking system collapsed and ecuador defaulted on its external debt later that year <\s>
<s> in march 2000 the congress approved a series of structural reforms that also provided for the adoption of the us dollar as legal tender <\s>
<s> dollarization stabilized the economy and positive growth returned in the years that followed helped by high oil prices remittances and increased non-traditional exports <\s>
<s> from 2002-06 the economy grew 5.5 the highest five-year average in 25 years <\s>
<s> after moderate growth in 2007 the economy reached a growth rate of 7.2 in 2008 in large part due to high global petroleum prices <\s>
